A margherita pizza was also very average, with a thin base, tomatoes all over it, and no cheese. I had never eaten a margherita like this before, and I didn‚Äôt even bother to take a photo.

Although it looks like the sea view is divided into two by the bathtub and the room from the photos, but In the end, I chose Westin, and the result did not disappoint, because there is a big balcony with a view of the sea. Sitting on the big sofa on the balcony, drinking beer and looking at the sea is not to mention how cool it is, even on sunny days. It is too hot to sit for a while, but it is still very comfortable to sit on the balcony after the sun goes down. And all the rooms in the hotel are facing the sea, no matter what type of room you book, you can see the sea, this is really well received, it is really an invincible sea view room. And when facing the sea, you can also see the coconut trees and swimming pools in the hotel park in front of you, forming a picture scroll with the sea and blue sky. Another important point is that you can see the invincible sea view while lying on the bed! ! ! This is really awesome.

Areas for improvement:
1. The breakfast in the hotel is a little simple. The western style is okay, but the Chinese food is not good, especially the steamed ones. There are only co**** grain staple foods, such as corn and sweet potatoes, and delicate snacks such as steamed chicken feet and steamed pork ribs. nothing. Chinese-style stir-fried dishes are also average, there is no desire to grab people's hands, and the colors and dishes are relatively simple.
2. You can put some beach chairs on the beach in front of the hotel. Now it is a bare beach with nothing. Although there is a sign stating that the sea area in front of the hotel is the open sea and you are not allowed to swim in the sea, you can still put some beach chairs. Let hotel guests sit on a beach chair and watch the ocean.
3. The hotel staff saw that the guests did not say hello 100% of the time, but a relatively small number of them said hello. The housekeeping department should say hello more frequently, because they will always meet in the corridor.
4. Takeaway can only be placed at the first gate of the hotel, which is where the vehicle lifts the pole. It is relatively dark at night after dark, and the lights in the park are not very bright. It is not convenient to pick up meals, and the takeaway staff will put them away He left on the ground, and asked him to wait for him. In fact, you can put a table a few meters away from the concierge desk at the entrance of the hotel for takeaway. Maybe the hotel thinks this will affect the image, but it is really inconvenient to take it so far away. The main reason is that it is too dark. Not so easy to spot...

However, even if it is the invincible sea view, it is really worth booking this hotel!
The lady at the front desk is very gentle and polite.
There is a little brother in the concierge department who is also very cheerful, that is, the taller and thinner one with the same hairstyle as the pot head.
When I checked out, I gave the hotel homemade biscuits as a souvenir, which was quite delicious.

Next time I go to Lingshui, I will choose to live in the Westin Blue Bay Greentown.
